Well, I don't know how the tab is going to look, since I only  
wrote it in Windows Notepad. But if you line up the chords  
and bars vertically, all the licks should fall into place.  
This song was originally played through a Leslie speaker,  
but sounds fine through a phaser or flanger.  
  
-----  
  
I've only tabbed the intro yet. The rest will follow later.  
The whole song is played with the guitar tuned down a half step.  
A Leslie is used to get the 'spacy sound'. This effect can be  
emulated with a chorus pedal at a medium slow rate.

Aw, shucks,  
If my daddy could see me now.  
  
Generally speaking Jimi rocks his pedal at a constant pace,  
like you would if you were tapping your foot with the music.  
The actual rhythm ebbs and flows and changes in a real jazzy  
way, so you'll need to listen the track. The chord change  
from B9 to C9 (and likewise from C#9 to D9) in particular  
changes in form and timing and is sometimes even omitted.  
So basically as with all tunes by improvisationally inspired  
artists best just to do your own thing!

Explanation of the musical symbols :  
7s9        slide from 7th fret to 9th  
7         slide from 7th fret down  
7/         slide from 7th fret up  
7bh        bend 7th and hold till ghost note or cb  
T          with thumb (E-string)  
7b         bend 7th 1 full step  
10v        vibrato 10th  
15bv       full bend and vibrato  
15cb       compound bend and release (every note picked) (full)  
3qb        bend 1/4step  
3wb        half bend
